4919 
4920 //------------------------------inline_arraycopy-----------------------
4921 // public static native void java.lang.System.arraycopy(Object src,  int  srcPos,
4922 //                                                      Object dest, int destPos,
4923 //                                                      int length);
4924 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_arraycopy() {
4925   // Get the arguments.
4926   Node* src         = argument(0);  // type: oop
4927   Node* src_offset  = argument(1);  // type: int
4928   Node* dest        = argument(2);  // type: oop
4929   Node* dest_offset = argument(3);  // type: int
4930   Node* length      = argument(4);  // type: int
4931 
4932   uint new_idx = C->unique();
4933 
4934   // Check for allocation before we add nodes that would confuse
4935   // tightly_coupled_allocation()
4936   AllocateArrayNode* alloc = tightly_coupled_allocation(dest, NULL);
4937 
4938   int saved_reexecute_sp = -1;
4939   JVMState* saved_jvms = arraycopy_restore_alloc_state(alloc, saved_reexecute_sp);
4940   // See arraycopy_restore_alloc_state() comment
4941   // if alloc == NULL we don't have to worry about a tightly coupled allocation so we can emit all needed guards
4942   // if saved_jvms != NULL (then alloc != NULL) then we can handle guards and a tightly coupled allocation
4943   // if saved_jvms == NULL and alloc != NULL, we can't emit any guards
4944   bool can_emit_guards = (alloc == NULL || saved_jvms != NULL);
4945 
4946   // The following tests must be performed
4947   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
4948   // (2) src and dest arrays must have elements of the same BasicType
4949   // (3) src and dest must not be null.
4950   // (4) src_offset must not be negative.
4951   // (5) dest_offset must not be negative.
4952   // (6) length must not be negative.
4953   // (7) src_offset + length must not exceed length of src.
4954   // (8) dest_offset + length must not exceed length of dest.
4955   // (9) each element of an oop array must be assignable
4956 
4957   // (3) src and dest must not be null.
4958   // always do this here because we need the JVM state for uncommon traps
4959   Node* null_ctl = top();
4960   src  = saved_jvms != NULL ? null_check_oop(src, &null_ctl, true, true) : null_check(src,  T_ARRAY);
4961   assert(null_ctl->is_top(), "no null control here");
4962   dest = null_check(dest, T_ARRAY);
4963 
4964   if (!can_emit_guards) {
4965     // if saved_jvms == NULL and alloc != NULL, we don't emit any
4966     // guards but the arraycopy node could still take advantage of a
4967     // tightly allocated allocation. tightly_coupled_allocation() is
4968     // called again to make sure it takes the null check above into
4969     // account: the null check is mandatory and if it caused an
4970     // uncommon trap to be emitted then the allocation can't be
4971     // considered tightly coupled in this context.
4972     alloc = tightly_coupled_allocation(dest, NULL);
4973   }
4974 
4975   bool validated = false;
4976 
4977   const Type* src_type  = _gvn.type(src);
4978   const Type* dest_type = _gvn.type(dest);
4979   const TypeAryPtr* top_src  = src_type->isa_aryptr();
4980   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
4981 
4982   // Do we have the type of src?
4983   bool has_src = (top_src != NULL && top_src->klass() != NULL);
4984   // Do we have the type of dest?
4985   bool has_dest = (top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL);
4986   // Is the type for src from speculation?
4987   bool src_spec = false;
4988   // Is the type for dest from speculation?
4989   bool dest_spec = false;
4990 
4991   if ((!has_src || !has_dest) && can_emit_guards) {
4992     // We don't have sufficient type information, let's see if
4993     // speculative types can help. We need to have types for both src
4994     // and dest so that it pays off.
4995 
4996     // Do we already have or could we have type information for src
4997     bool could_have_src = has_src;
4998     // Do we already have or could we have type information for dest
4999     bool could_have_dest = has_dest;
5000 
5001     ciKlass* src_k = NULL;
5002     if (!has_src) {
5003       src_k = src_type->speculative_type_not_null();
5004       if (src_k != NULL && src_k->is_array_klass()) {
5005         could_have_src = true;
5006       }
5007     }
5008 
5009     ciKlass* dest_k = NULL;
5010     if (!has_dest) {
5011       dest_k = dest_type->speculative_type_not_null();
5012       if (dest_k != NULL && dest_k->is_array_klass()) {
5013         could_have_dest = true;
5014       }
5015     }
5016 
5017     if (could_have_src && could_have_dest) {
5018       // This is going to pay off so emit the required guards
5019       if (!has_src) {
5020         src = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(src, src_k, true);
5021         src_type  = _gvn.type(src);
5022         top_src  = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5023         has_src = (top_src != NULL && top_src->klass() != NULL);
5024         src_spec = true;
5025       }
5026       if (!has_dest) {
5027         dest = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(dest, dest_k, true);
5028         dest_type  = _gvn.type(dest);
5029         top_dest  = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
5030         has_dest = (top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL);
5031         dest_spec = true;
5032       }
5033     }
5034   }
5035 
5036   if (has_src && has_dest && can_emit_guards) {
5037     BasicType src_elem  = top_src->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5038     BasicType dest_elem = top_dest->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5039     if (src_elem  == T_ARRAY)  src_elem  = T_OBJECT;
5040     if (dest_elem == T_ARRAY)  dest_elem = T_OBJECT;
5041 
5042     if (src_elem == dest_elem && src_elem == T_OBJECT) {
5043       // If both arrays are object arrays then having the exact types
5044       // for both will remove the need for a subtype check at runtime
5045       // before the call and may make it possible to pick a faster copy
5046       // routine (without a subtype check on every element)
5047       // Do we have the exact type of src?
5048       bool could_have_src = src_spec;
5049       // Do we have the exact type of dest?
5050       bool could_have_dest = dest_spec;
5051       ciKlass* src_k = top_src->klass();
5052       ciKlass* dest_k = top_dest->klass();
5053       if (!src_spec) {
5054         src_k = src_type->speculative_type_not_null();
5055         if (src_k != NULL && src_k->is_array_klass()) {
5056           could_have_src = true;
5057         }
5058       }
5059       if (!dest_spec) {
5060         dest_k = dest_type->speculative_type_not_null();
5061         if (dest_k != NULL && dest_k->is_array_klass()) {
5062           could_have_dest = true;
5063         }
5064       }
5065       if (could_have_src && could_have_dest) {
5066         // If we can have both exact types, emit the missing guards
5067         if (could_have_src && !src_spec) {
5068           src = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(src, src_k, true);
5069         }
5070         if (could_have_dest && !dest_spec) {
5071           dest = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(dest, dest_k, true);
5072         }
5073       }
5074     }
5075   }
5076 
5077   ciMethod* trap_method = method();
5078   int trap_bci = bci();
5079   if (saved_jvms != NULL) {
5080     trap_method = alloc->jvms()->method();
5081     trap_bci = alloc->jvms()->bci();
5082   }
5083 
5084   bool negative_length_guard_generated = false;
5085 
5086   if (!C->too_many_traps(trap_method, trap_bci, Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic) &&
5087       can_emit_guards &&
5088       !src->is_top() && !dest->is_top()) {
5089     // validate arguments: enables transformation the ArrayCopyNode
5090     validated = true;
5091 
5092     RegionNode* slow_region = new RegionNode(1);
5093     record_for_igvn(slow_region);
5094 
5095     // (1) src and dest are arrays.
5096     generate_non_array_guard(load_object_klass(src), slow_region);
5097     generate_non_array_guard(load_object_klass(dest), slow_region);
5098 
5099     // (2) src and dest arrays must have elements of the same BasicType
5100     // done at macro expansion or at Ideal transformation time
5101 
5102     // (4) src_offset must not be negative.
5103     generate_negative_guard(src_offset, slow_region);
5104 
5105     // (5) dest_offset must not be negative.
5106     generate_negative_guard(dest_offset, slow_region);
5107 
5108     // (7) src_offset + length must not exceed length of src.
5109     generate_limit_guard(src_offset, length,
5110                          load_array_length(src),
5111                          slow_region);
5112 
5113     // (8) dest_offset + length must not exceed length of dest.
5114     generate_limit_guard(dest_offset, length,
5115                          load_array_length(dest),
5116                          slow_region);
5117 
5118     // (6) length must not be negative.
5119     // This is also checked in generate_arraycopy() during macro expansion, but
5120     // we also have to check it here for the case where the ArrayCopyNode will
5121     // be eliminated by Escape Analysis.
5122     if (EliminateAllocations) {
5123       generate_negative_guard(length, slow_region);
5124       negative_length_guard_generated = true;
5125     }
5126 
5127     // (9) each element of an oop array must be assignable
5128     Node* dest_klass = load_object_klass(dest);
5129     if (src != dest) {
5130       Node* not_subtype_ctrl = gen_subtype_check(src, dest_klass);
5131 
5132       if (not_subtype_ctrl != top()) {
5133         PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
5134         set_control(not_subtype_ctrl);
5135         uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
5136                       Deoptimization::Action_make_not_entrant);
5137         assert(stopped(), "Should be stopped");
5138       }
5139     }
5140 
5141     const TypeKlassPtr* dest_klass_t = _gvn.type(dest_klass)->is_klassptr();
5142     const Type* toop = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(dest_klass_t->klass());
5143     src = _gvn.transform(new CheckCastPPNode(control(), src, toop));
5144     src_type = _gvn.type(src);
5145     top_src  = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5146 
5147     if (top_dest != NULL && !top_dest->elem()->isa_valuetype() && !top_dest->is_not_flat()) {
5148       generate_valueArray_guard(dest_klass, slow_region);
5149     }
5150 
5151     if (top_src != NULL && !top_src->elem()->isa_valuetype() && !top_src->is_not_flat()) {
5152       Node* src_klass = load_object_klass(src);
5153       generate_valueArray_guard(src_klass, slow_region);
5154     }
5155 
5156     {
5157       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
5158       set_control(_gvn.transform(slow_region));
5159       uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
5160                     Deoptimization::Action_make_not_entrant);
5161       assert(stopped(), "Should be stopped");
5162     }
5163   }
5164 
5165   arraycopy_move_allocation_here(alloc, dest, saved_jvms, saved_reexecute_sp, new_idx);
5166 
5167   if (stopped()) {
5168     return true;
5169   }
5170 
5171   ArrayCopyNode* ac = ArrayCopyNode::make(this, true, src, src_offset, dest, dest_offset, length, alloc != NULL, negative_length_guard_generated,
5172                                           // Create LoadRange and LoadKlass nodes for use during macro expansion here
5173                                           // so the compiler has a chance to eliminate them: during macro expansion,
5174                                           // we have to set their control (CastPP nodes are eliminated).
5175                                           load_object_klass(src), load_object_klass(dest),
5176                                           load_array_length(src), load_array_length(dest));
5177 
5178   ac->set_arraycopy(validated);
5179 
5180   Node* n = _gvn.transform(ac);
5181   if (n == ac) {
5182     ac->connect_outputs(this);
5183   } else {
5184     assert(validated, "shouldn't transform if all arguments not validated");
5185     set_all_memory(n);
5186   }
5187   clear_upper_avx();
5188 
5189 
5190   return true;
5191 }
5192 
5193 
5194 // Helper function which determines if an arraycopy immediately follows
5195 // an allocation, with no intervening tests or other escapes for the object.
5196 AllocateArrayNode*
5197 LibraryCallKit::tightly_coupled_allocation(Node* ptr,
5198                                            RegionNode* slow_region) {
5199   if (stopped())             return NULL;  // no fast path
5200   if (C->AliasLevel() == 0)  return NULL;  // no MergeMems around
5201 
5202   AllocateArrayNode* alloc = AllocateArrayNode::Ideal_array_allocation(ptr, &_gvn);
5203   if (alloc == NULL)  return NULL;
5204 
5205   Node* rawmem = memory(Compile::AliasIdxRaw);
5206   // Is the allocation's memory state untouched?
5207   if (!(rawmem->is_Proj() && rawmem->in(0)->is_Initialize())) {
5208     // Bail out if there have been raw-memory effects since the allocation.
5209     // (Example:  There might have been a call or safepoint.)
5210     return NULL;
5211   }
5212   rawmem = rawmem->in(0)->as_Initialize()->memory(Compile::AliasIdxRaw);
5213   if (!(rawmem->is_Proj() && rawmem->in(0) == alloc)) {
5214     return NULL;
5215   }
5216 
5217   // There must be no unexpected observers of this allocation.
5218   for (DUIterator_Fast imax, i = ptr->fast_outs(imax); i < imax; i++) {
5219     Node* obs = ptr->fast_out(i);
5220     if (obs != this->map()) {
5221       return NULL;
5222     }
5223   }
5224 
5225   // This arraycopy must unconditionally follow the allocation of the ptr.
5226   Node* alloc_ctl = ptr->in(0);
5227   Node* ctl = control();
5228   while (ctl != alloc_ctl) {
5229     // There may be guards which feed into the slow_region.
5230     // Any other control flow means that we might not get a chance
5231     // to finish initializing the allocated object.
5232     if ((ctl->is_IfFalse() || ctl->is_IfTrue()) && ctl->in(0)->is_If()) {
5233       IfNode* iff = ctl->in(0)->as_If();
5234       Node* not_ctl = iff->proj_out_or_null(1 - ctl->as_Proj()->_con);
5235       assert(not_ctl != NULL && not_ctl != ctl, "found alternate");
5236       if (slow_region != NULL && slow_region->find_edge(not_ctl) >= 1) {
5237         ctl = iff->in(0);       // This test feeds the known slow_region.
5238         continue;
5239       }
5240       // One more try:  Various low-level checks bottom out in
5241       // uncommon traps.  If the debug-info of the trap omits
5242       // any reference to the allocation, as we've already
5243       // observed, then there can be no objection to the trap.
5244       bool found_trap = false;
5245       for (DUIterator_Fast jmax, j = not_ctl->fast_outs(jmax); j < jmax; j++) {
5246         Node* obs = not_ctl->fast_out(j);
5247         if (obs->in(0) == not_ctl && obs->is_Call() &&
5248             (obs->as_Call()->entry_point() == SharedRuntime::uncommon_trap_blob()->entry_point())) {
5249           found_trap = true; break;
5250         }
5251       }
5252       if (found_trap) {
5253         ctl = iff->in(0);       // This test feeds a harmless uncommon trap.
5254         continue;
5255       }
5256     }
5257     return NULL;
5258   }
5259 
5260   // If we get this far, we have an allocation which immediately
5261   // precedes the arraycopy, and we can take over zeroing the new object.
5262   // The arraycopy will finish the initialization, and provide
5263   // a new control state to which we will anchor the destination pointer.
5264 
5265   return alloc;
5266 }
5267 
5268 //-------------inline_encodeISOArray-----------------------------------
5269 // encode char[] to byte[] in ISO_8859_1
5270 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_encodeISOArray() {
5271   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "encodeISOArray has 5 parameters");
5272   // no receiver since it is static method
5273   Node *src         = argument(0);
5274   Node *src_offset  = argument(1);
5275   Node *dst         = argument(2);
5276   Node *dst_offset  = argument(3);
5277   Node *length      = argument(4);
5278 
5279   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
5280   dst = must_be_not_null(dst, true);
5281 
5282   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5283   const Type* dst_type = dst->Value(&_gvn);
5284   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5285   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dst_type->isa_aryptr();
5286   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL ||
5287       top_dest == NULL || top_dest->klass() == NULL) {
5288     // failed array check
5289     return false;
5290   }
5291 
5292   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
5293   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5294   BasicType dst_elem = dst_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5295   if (!((src_elem == T_CHAR) || (src_elem== T_BYTE)) || dst_elem != T_BYTE) {
5296     return false;
5297   }
5298 
5299   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, src_offset, T_CHAR);
5300   Node* dst_start = array_element_address(dst, dst_offset, dst_elem);
5301   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5302   // 'dst_start' points to dst array + scaled offset
5303 
5304   const TypeAryPtr* mtype = TypeAryPtr::BYTES;
5305   Node* enc = new EncodeISOArrayNode(control(), memory(mtype), src_start, dst_start, length);
5306   enc = _gvn.transform(enc);
5307   Node* res_mem = _gvn.transform(new SCMemProjNode(enc));
5308   set_memory(res_mem, mtype);
5309   set_result(enc);
5310   clear_upper_avx();
5311 
5312   return true;
5313 }
5314 
5315 //-------------inline_multiplyToLen-----------------------------------
5316 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_multiplyToLen() {
5317   assert(UseMultiplyToLenIntrinsic, "not implemented on this platform");
5318 
5319   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::multiplyToLen();
5320   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5321     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5322   }
5323   const char* stubName = "multiplyToLen";
5324 
5325   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "multiplyToLen has 5 parameters");
5326 
5327   // no receiver because it is a static method
5328   Node* x    = argument(0);
5329   Node* xlen = argument(1);
5330   Node* y    = argument(2);
5331   Node* ylen = argument(3);
5332   Node* z    = argument(4);
5333 
5334   x = must_be_not_null(x, true);
5335   y = must_be_not_null(y, true);
5336 
5337   const Type* x_type = x->Value(&_gvn);
5338   const Type* y_type = y->Value(&_gvn);
5339   const TypeAryPtr* top_x = x_type->isa_aryptr();
5340   const TypeAryPtr* top_y = y_type->isa_aryptr();
5341   if (top_x  == NULL || top_x->klass()  == NULL ||
5342       top_y == NULL || top_y->klass() == NULL) {
5343     // failed array check
5344     return false;
5345   }
5346 
5347   BasicType x_elem = x_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5348   BasicType y_elem = y_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5349   if (x_elem != T_INT || y_elem != T_INT) {
5350     return false;
5351   }
5352 
5353   // Set the original stack and the reexecute bit for the interpreter to reexecute
5354   // the bytecode that invokes BigInteger.multiplyToLen() if deoptimization happens
5355   // on the return from z array allocation in runtime.
5356   { PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
5357     jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
5358 
5359     Node* x_start = array_element_address(x, intcon(0), x_elem);
5360     Node* y_start = array_element_address(y, intcon(0), y_elem);
5361     // 'x_start' points to x array + scaled xlen
5362     // 'y_start' points to y array + scaled ylen
5363 
5364     // Allocate the result array
5365     Node* zlen = _gvn.transform(new AddINode(xlen, ylen));
5366     ciKlass* klass = ciTypeArrayKlass::make(T_INT);
5367     Node* klass_node = makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(klass));
5368 
5369     IdealKit ideal(this);
5370 
5371 #define __ ideal.
5372      Node* one = __ ConI(1);
5373      Node* zero = __ ConI(0);
5374      IdealVariable need_alloc(ideal), z_alloc(ideal);  __ declarations_done();
5375      __ set(need_alloc, zero);
5376      __ set(z_alloc, z);
5377      __ if_then(z, BoolTest::eq, null()); {
5378        __ increment (need_alloc, one);
5379      } __ else_(); {
5380        // Update graphKit memory and control from IdealKit.
5381        sync_kit(ideal);
5382        Node *cast = new CastPPNode(z, TypePtr::NOTNULL);
5383        cast->init_req(0, control());
5384        _gvn.set_type(cast, cast->bottom_type());
5385        C->record_for_igvn(cast);
5386 
5387        Node* zlen_arg = load_array_length(cast);
5388        // Update IdealKit memory and control from graphKit.
5389        __ sync_kit(this);
5390        __ if_then(zlen_arg, BoolTest::lt, zlen); {
5391          __ increment (need_alloc, one);
5392        } __ end_if();
5393      } __ end_if();
5394 
5395      __ if_then(__ value(need_alloc), BoolTest::ne, zero); {
5396        // Update graphKit memory and control from IdealKit.
5397        sync_kit(ideal);
5398        Node * narr = new_array(klass_node, zlen, 1);
5399        // Update IdealKit memory and control from graphKit.
5400        __ sync_kit(this);
5401        __ set(z_alloc, narr);
5402      } __ end_if();
5403 
5404      sync_kit(ideal);
5405      z = __ value(z_alloc);
5406      // Can't use TypeAryPtr::INTS which uses Bottom offset.
5407      _gvn.set_type(z, TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(klass));
5408      // Final sync IdealKit and GraphKit.
5409      final_sync(ideal);
5410 #undef __
5411 
5412     Node* z_start = array_element_address(z, intcon(0), T_INT);
5413 
5414     Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
5415                                    OptoRuntime::multiplyToLen_Type(),
5416                                    stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5417                                    x_start, xlen, y_start, ylen, z_start, zlen);
5418   } // original reexecute is set back here
5419 
5420   C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
5421   set_result(z);
5422   return true;
5423 }
5424 
5425 //-------------inline_squareToLen------------------------------------
5426 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_squareToLen() {
5427   assert(UseSquareToLenIntrinsic, "not implemented on this platform");
5428 
5429   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::squareToLen();
5430   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5431     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5432   }
5433   const char* stubName = "squareToLen";
5434 
5435   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "implSquareToLen has 4 parameters");
5436 
5437   Node* x    = argument(0);
5438   Node* len  = argument(1);
5439   Node* z    = argument(2);
5440   Node* zlen = argument(3);
5441 
5442   x = must_be_not_null(x, true);
5443   z = must_be_not_null(z, true);
5444 
5445   const Type* x_type = x->Value(&_gvn);
5446   const Type* z_type = z->Value(&_gvn);
5447   const TypeAryPtr* top_x = x_type->isa_aryptr();
5448   const TypeAryPtr* top_z = z_type->isa_aryptr();
5449   if (top_x  == NULL || top_x->klass()  == NULL ||
5450       top_z  == NULL || top_z->klass()  == NULL) {
5451     // failed array check
5452     return false;
5453   }
5454 
5455   BasicType x_elem = x_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5456   BasicType z_elem = z_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5457   if (x_elem != T_INT || z_elem != T_INT) {
5458     return false;
5459   }
5460 
5461 
5462   Node* x_start = array_element_address(x, intcon(0), x_elem);
5463   Node* z_start = array_element_address(z, intcon(0), z_elem);
5464 
5465   Node*  call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
5466                                   OptoRuntime::squareToLen_Type(),
5467                                   stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5468                                   x_start, len, z_start, zlen);
5469 
5470   set_result(z);
5471   return true;
5472 }

5474 //-------------inline_mulAdd------------------------------------------
5475 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_mulAdd() {
5476   assert(UseMulAddIntrinsic, "not implemented on this platform");
5477 
5478   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::mulAdd();
5479   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5480     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5481   }
5482   const char* stubName = "mulAdd";
5483 
5484   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "mulAdd has 5 parameters");
5485 
5486   Node* out      = argument(0);
5487   Node* in       = argument(1);
5488   Node* offset   = argument(2);
5489   Node* len      = argument(3);
5490   Node* k        = argument(4);
5491 
5492   out = must_be_not_null(out, true);
5493 
5494   const Type* out_type = out->Value(&_gvn);
5495   const Type* in_type = in->Value(&_gvn);
5496   const TypeAryPtr* top_out = out_type->isa_aryptr();
5497   const TypeAryPtr* top_in = in_type->isa_aryptr();
5498   if (top_out  == NULL || top_out->klass()  == NULL ||
5499       top_in == NULL || top_in->klass() == NULL) {
5500     // failed array check
5501     return false;
5502   }
5503 
5504   BasicType out_elem = out_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5505   BasicType in_elem = in_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5506   if (out_elem != T_INT || in_elem != T_INT) {
5507     return false;
5508   }
5509 
5510   Node* outlen = load_array_length(out);
5511   Node* new_offset = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(outlen, offset));
5512   Node* out_start = array_element_address(out, intcon(0), out_elem);
5513   Node* in_start = array_element_address(in, intcon(0), in_elem);
5514 
5515   Node*  call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
5516                                   OptoRuntime::mulAdd_Type(),
5517                                   stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5518                                   out_start,in_start, new_offset, len, k);
5519   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5520   set_result(result);
5521   return true;
5522 }

5524 //-------------inline_montgomeryMultiply-----------------------------------
5525 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_montgomeryMultiply() {
5526   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::montgomeryMultiply();
5527   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5528     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5529   }
5530 
5531   assert(UseMontgomeryMultiplyIntrinsic, "not implemented on this platform");
5532   const char* stubName = "montgomery_multiply";
5533 
5534   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 7, "montgomeryMultiply has 7 parameters");
5535 
5536   Node* a    = argument(0);
5537   Node* b    = argument(1);
5538   Node* n    = argument(2);
5539   Node* len  = argument(3);
5540   Node* inv  = argument(4);
5541   Node* m    = argument(6);
5542 
5543   const Type* a_type = a->Value(&_gvn);
5544   const TypeAryPtr* top_a = a_type->isa_aryptr();
5545   const Type* b_type = b->Value(&_gvn);
5546   const TypeAryPtr* top_b = b_type->isa_aryptr();
5547   const Type* n_type = a->Value(&_gvn);
5548   const TypeAryPtr* top_n = n_type->isa_aryptr();
5549   const Type* m_type = a->Value(&_gvn);
5550   const TypeAryPtr* top_m = m_type->isa_aryptr();
5551   if (top_a  == NULL || top_a->klass()  == NULL ||
5552       top_b == NULL || top_b->klass()  == NULL ||
5553       top_n == NULL || top_n->klass()  == NULL ||
5554       top_m == NULL || top_m->klass()  == NULL) {
5555     // failed array check
5556     return false;
5557   }
5558 
5559   BasicType a_elem = a_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5560   BasicType b_elem = b_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5561   BasicType n_elem = n_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5562   BasicType m_elem = m_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5563   if (a_elem != T_INT || b_elem != T_INT || n_elem != T_INT || m_elem != T_INT) {
5564     return false;
5565   }
5566 
5567   // Make the call
5568   {
5569     Node* a_start = array_element_address(a, intcon(0), a_elem);
5570     Node* b_start = array_element_address(b, intcon(0), b_elem);
5571     Node* n_start = array_element_address(n, intcon(0), n_elem);
5572     Node* m_start = array_element_address(m, intcon(0), m_elem);
5573 
5574     Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF,
5575                                    OptoRuntime::montgomeryMultiply_Type(),
5576                                    stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5577                                    a_start, b_start, n_start, len, inv, top(),
5578                                    m_start);
5579     set_result(m);
5580   }
5581 
5582   return true;
5583 }

5639 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_bigIntegerShift(bool isRightShift) {
5640   address stubAddr = NULL;
5641   const char* stubName = NULL;
5642 
5643   stubAddr = isRightShift? StubRoutines::bigIntegerRightShift(): StubRoutines::bigIntegerLeftShift();
5644   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5645     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5646   }
5647 
5648   stubName = isRightShift? "bigIntegerRightShiftWorker" : "bigIntegerLeftShiftWorker";
5649 
5650   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "expected 5 arguments");
5651 
5652   Node* newArr = argument(0);
5653   Node* oldArr = argument(1);
5654   Node* newIdx = argument(2);
5655   Node* shiftCount = argument(3);
5656   Node* numIter = argument(4);
5657 
5658   const Type* newArr_type = newArr->Value(&_gvn);
5659   const TypeAryPtr* top_newArr = newArr_type->isa_aryptr();
5660   const Type* oldArr_type = oldArr->Value(&_gvn);
5661   const TypeAryPtr* top_oldArr = oldArr_type->isa_aryptr();
5662   if (top_newArr == NULL || top_newArr->klass() == NULL || top_oldArr == NULL
5663       || top_oldArr->klass() == NULL) {
5664     return false;
5665   }
5666 
5667   BasicType newArr_elem = newArr_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5668   BasicType oldArr_elem = oldArr_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5669   if (newArr_elem != T_INT || oldArr_elem != T_INT) {
5670     return false;
5671   }
5672 
5673   // Make the call
5674   {
5675     Node* newArr_start = array_element_address(newArr, intcon(0), newArr_elem);
5676     Node* oldArr_start = array_element_address(oldArr, intcon(0), oldArr_elem);
5677 
5678     Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF,
5679                                    OptoRuntime::bigIntegerShift_Type(),
5680                                    stubAddr,
5681                                    stubName,
5682                                    TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5683                                    newArr_start,
5684                                    oldArr_start,
5685                                    newIdx,
5686                                    shiftCount,
5687                                    numIter);
5688   }
5689 
5690   return true;
5691 }

5698   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5699     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5700   }

5702   int size_l = callee()->signature()->size();
5703   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 8, "vectorizedMismatch has 6 parameters");
5704 
5705   Node* obja = argument(0);

5707   Node* objb = argument(3);
5708   Node* boffset = argument(4);

5738 /**
5739  * Calculate CRC32 for byte.
5740  * int java.util.zip.CRC32.update(int crc, int b)
5741  */
5742 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateCRC32() {
5743   assert(UseCRC32Intrinsics, "need AVX and LCMUL instructions support");
5744   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 2, "update has 2 parameters");
5745   // no receiver since it is static method
5746   Node* crc  = argument(0); // type: int
5747   Node* b    = argument(1); // type: int
5748 
5749   /*
5750    *    int c = ~ crc;
5751    *    b = timesXtoThe32[(b ^ c) & 0xFF];
5752    *    b = b ^ (c >>> 8);
5753    *    crc = ~b;
5754    */
5755 
5756   Node* M1 = intcon(-1);
5757   crc = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(crc, M1));
5758   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(crc, b));
5759   result = _gvn.transform(new AndINode(result, intcon(0xFF)));
5760 
5761   Node* base = makecon(TypeRawPtr::make(StubRoutines::crc_table_addr()));
5762   Node* offset = _gvn.transform(new LShiftINode(result, intcon(0x2)));
5763   Node* adr = basic_plus_adr(top(), base, ConvI2X(offset));
5764   result = make_load(control(), adr, TypeInt::INT, T_INT, MemNode::unordered);
5765 
5766   crc = _gvn.transform(new URShiftINode(crc, intcon(8)));
5767   result = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(crc, result));
5768   result = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(result, M1));
5769   set_result(result);
5770   return true;
5771 }
5772 
5773 /**
5774  * Calculate CRC32 for byte[] array.
5775  * int java.util.zip.CRC32.updateBytes(int crc, byte[] buf, int off, int len)
5776  */
5777 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateBytesCRC32() {
5778   assert(UseCRC32Intrinsics, "need AVX and LCMUL instructions support");
5779   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "updateBytes has 4 parameters");
5780   // no receiver since it is static method
5781   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5782   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: oop
5783   Node* offset  = argument(2); // type: int
5784   Node* length  = argument(3); // type: int
5785 
5786   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5787   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5788   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
5789     // failed array check
5790     return false;
5791   }
5792 
5793   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
5794   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5795   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
5796     return false;
5797   }
5798 
5799   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5800   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
5801   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, offset, src_elem);
5802 
5803   // We assume that range check is done by caller.
5804   // TODO: generate range check (offset+length < src.length) in debug VM.
5805 
5806   // Call the stub.
5807   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesCRC32();
5808   const char *stubName = "updateBytesCRC32";
5809 
5810   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::updateBytesCRC32_Type(),
5811                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5812                                  crc, src_start, length);
5813   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5814   set_result(result);
5815   return true;
5816 }

5818 /**
5819  * Calculate CRC32 for ByteBuffer.
5820  * int java.util.zip.CRC32.updateByteBuffer(int crc, long buf, int off, int len)
5821  */
5822 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateByteBufferCRC32() {
5823   assert(UseCRC32Intrinsics, "need AVX and LCMUL instructions support");
5824   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "updateByteBuffer has 4 parameters and one is long");
5825   // no receiver since it is static method
5826   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5827   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: long
5828   Node* offset  = argument(3); // type: int
5829   Node* length  = argument(4); // type: int
5830 
5831   src = ConvL2X(src);  // adjust Java long to machine word
5832   Node* base = _gvn.transform(new CastX2PNode(src));
5833   offset = ConvI2X(offset);
5834 
5835   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5836   Node* src_start = basic_plus_adr(top(), base, offset);
5837 
5838   // Call the stub.
5839   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesCRC32();
5840   const char *stubName = "updateBytesCRC32";
5841 
5842   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::updateBytesCRC32_Type(),
5843                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5844                                  crc, src_start, length);
5845   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5846   set_result(result);
5847   return true;
5848 }

5850 //------------------------------get_table_from_crc32c_class-----------------------
5851 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_table_from_crc32c_class(ciInstanceKlass *crc32c_class) {
5852   Node* table = load_field_from_object(NULL, "byteTable", "[I", /*is_exact*/ false, /*is_static*/ true, crc32c_class);
5853   assert (table != NULL, "wrong version of java.util.zip.CRC32C");
5854 
5855   return table;
5856 }

5863 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateBytesCRC32C() {

5867   // no receiver since it is a static method
5868   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5869   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: oop
5870   Node* offset  = argument(2); // type: int
5871   Node* end     = argument(3); // type: int
5872 
5873   Node* length = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(end, offset));
5874 
5875   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5876   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();

5878     // failed array check

5958 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateBytesAdler32() {
5959   assert(UseAdler32Intrinsics, "Adler32 Instrinsic support need"); // check if we actually need to check this flag or check a different one
5960   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "updateBytes has 4 parameters");
5961   assert(callee()->holder()->is_loaded(), "Adler32 class must be loaded");
5962   // no receiver since it is static method
5963   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5964   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: oop
5965   Node* offset  = argument(2); // type: int
5966   Node* length  = argument(3); // type: int
5967 
5968   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5969   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5970   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
5971     // failed array check
5972     return false;
5973   }
5974 
5975   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
5976   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5977   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
5978     return false;
5979   }
5980 
5981   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5982   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, offset, src_elem);
5983 
5984   // We assume that range check is done by caller.
5985   // TODO: generate range check (offset+length < src.length) in debug VM.
5986 
5987   // Call the stub.
5988   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesAdler32();
5989   const char *stubName = "updateBytesAdler32";
5990 
5991   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF, OptoRuntime::updateBytesAdler32_Type(),
5992                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5993                                  crc, src_start, length);
5994   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5995   set_result(result);
5996   return true;
5997 }
5998 
5999 //------------------------------inline_updateByteBufferAdler32---------------
6000 //
6001 // Calculate Adler32 checksum for DirectByteBuffer.
6002 // int java.util.zip.Adler32.updateByteBuffer(int crc, long buf, int off, int len)
6003 //
6004 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateByteBufferAdler32() {
6005   assert(UseAdler32Intrinsics, "Adler32 Instrinsic support need"); // check if we actually need to check this flag or check a different one
6006   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "updateByteBuffer has 4 parameters and one is long");
6007   assert(callee()->holder()->is_loaded(), "Adler32 class must be loaded");
6008   // no receiver since it is static method
6009   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
6010   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: long
6011   Node* offset  = argument(3); // type: int
6012   Node* length  = argument(4); // type: int
6013 
6014   src = ConvL2X(src);  // adjust Java long to machine word
6015   Node* base = _gvn.transform(new CastX2PNode(src));
6016   offset = ConvI2X(offset);
6017 
6018   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
6019   Node* src_start = basic_plus_adr(top(), base, offset);
6020 
6021   // Call the stub.
6022   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesAdler32();
6023   const char *stubName = "updateBytesAdler32";
6024 
6025   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF, OptoRuntime::updateBytesAdler32_Type(),
6026                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6027                                  crc, src_start, length);
6028 
6029   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
6030   set_result(result);
6031   return true;
6032 }
6033 
6034 //----------------------------inline_reference_get----------------------------
6035 // public T java.lang.ref.Reference.get();
6036 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_reference_get() {
6037   const int referent_offset = java_lang_ref_Reference::referent_offset();
6038 
6039   // Get the argument:
6040   Node* reference_obj = null_check_receiver();
6041   if (stopped()) return true;
6042 
6043   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(reference_obj)->isa_instptr();
6044   assert(tinst != NULL, "obj is null");
6045   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "obj is not loaded");
6046   ciInstanceKlass* referenceKlass = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass();
6047   ciField* field = referenceKlass->get_field_by_name(ciSymbol::make("referent"),
6048                                                      ciSymbol::make("Ljava/lang/Object;"),
6049                                                      false);
6050   assert (field != NULL, "undefined field");
6051 
6052   Node* adr = basic_plus_adr(reference_obj, reference_obj, referent_offset);
6053   const TypePtr* adr_type = C->alias_type(field)->adr_type();
6054 
6055   ciInstanceKlass* klass = env()->Object_klass();
6056   const TypeOopPtr* object_type = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(klass);
6057 
6058   DecoratorSet decorators = IN_HEAP | ON_WEAK_OOP_REF;
6059   Node* result = access_load_at(reference_obj, adr, adr_type, object_type, T_OBJECT, decorators);
6060   // Add memory barrier to prevent commoning reads from this field
6061   // across safepoint since GC can change its value.
6062   insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
6063 
6064   set_result(result);
6065   return true;
6066 }
6067 
6068 
6069 Node * LibraryCallKit::load_field_from_object(Node * fromObj, const char * fieldName, const char * fieldTypeString,
6070                                               bool is_exact=true, bool is_static=false,
6071                                               ciInstanceKlass * fromKls=NULL) {
6072   if (fromKls == NULL) {
6073     const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(fromObj)->isa_instptr();
6074     assert(tinst != NULL, "obj is null");
6075     assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "obj is not loaded");
6076     assert(!is_exact || tinst->klass_is_exact(), "klass not exact");
6077     fromKls = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass();
6078   } else {
6079     assert(is_static, "only for static field access");
6080   }
6081   ciField* field = fromKls->get_field_by_name(ciSymbol::make(fieldName),
6082                                               ciSymbol::make(fieldTypeString),
6083                                               is_static);
6084 
6085   assert (field != NULL, "undefined field");
6086   if (field == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6087 
6088   if (is_static) {
6089     const TypeInstPtr* tip = TypeInstPtr::make(fromKls->java_mirror());
6090     fromObj = makecon(tip);
6091   }
6092 
6093   // Next code  copied from Parse::do_get_xxx():
6094 
6095   // Compute address and memory type.
6096   int offset  = field->offset_in_bytes();
6097   bool is_vol = field->is_volatile();
6098   ciType* field_klass = field->type();
6099   assert(field_klass->is_loaded(), "should be loaded");
6100   const TypePtr* adr_type = C->alias_type(field)->adr_type();
6101   Node *adr = basic_plus_adr(fromObj, fromObj, offset);
6102   BasicType bt = field->layout_type();
6103 
6104   // Build the resultant type of the load
6105   const Type *type;
6106   if (bt == T_OBJECT) {
6107     type = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(field_klass->as_klass());
6108   } else {
6109     type = Type::get_const_basic_type(bt);
6110   }
6111 
6112   DecoratorSet decorators = IN_HEAP;
6113 
6114   if (is_vol) {
6115     decorators |= MO_SEQ_CST;
6116   }
6117 
6118   return access_load_at(fromObj, adr, adr_type, type, bt, decorators);
6119 }
6120 
6121 Node * LibraryCallKit::field_address_from_object(Node * fromObj, const char * fieldName, const char * fieldTypeString,
6122                                                  bool is_exact = true, bool is_static = false,
6123                                                  ciInstanceKlass * fromKls = NULL) {
6124   if (fromKls == NULL) {
6125     const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(fromObj)->isa_instptr();
6126     assert(tinst != NULL, "obj is null");
6127     assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "obj is not loaded");
6128     assert(!is_exact || tinst->klass_is_exact(), "klass not exact");
6129     fromKls = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass();
6130   }
6131   else {
6132     assert(is_static, "only for static field access");
6133   }
6134   ciField* field = fromKls->get_field_by_name(ciSymbol::make(fieldName),
6135     ciSymbol::make(fieldTypeString),
6136     is_static);
6137 
6138   assert(field != NULL, "undefined field");
6139   assert(!field->is_volatile(), "not defined for volatile fields");
6140 
6141   if (is_static) {
6142     const TypeInstPtr* tip = TypeInstPtr::make(fromKls->java_mirror());
6143     fromObj = makecon(tip);
6144   }
6145 
6146   // Next code  copied from Parse::do_get_xxx():
6147 
6148   // Compute address and memory type.
6149   int offset = field->offset_in_bytes();
6150   Node *adr = basic_plus_adr(fromObj, fromObj, offset);
6151 
6152   return adr;
6153 }

6155 //------------------------------inline_aescrypt_Block-----------------------
6156 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_aescrypt_Block(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6157   address stubAddr = NULL;
6158   const char *stubName;
6159   assert(UseAES, "need AES instruction support");
6160 
6161   switch(id) {
6162   case vmIntrinsics::_aescrypt_encryptBlock:
6163     stubAddr = StubRoutines::aescrypt_encryptBlock();
6164     stubName = "aescrypt_encryptBlock";
6165     break;
6166   case vmIntrinsics::_aescrypt_decryptBlock:
6167     stubAddr = StubRoutines::aescrypt_decryptBlock();
6168     stubName = "aescrypt_decryptBlock";
6169     break;
6170   default:
6171     break;
6172   }
6173   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6174 
6175   Node* aescrypt_object = argument(0);
6176   Node* src             = argument(1);
6177   Node* src_offset      = argument(2);
6178   Node* dest            = argument(3);
6179   Node* dest_offset     = argument(4);
6180 
6181   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
6182   dest = must_be_not_null(dest, true);
6183 
6184   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
6185   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6186   const Type* dest_type = dest->Value(&_gvn);
6187   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6188   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
6189   assert (top_src  != NULL && top_src->klass()  != NULL &&  top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL, "args are strange");
6190 
6191   // for the quick and dirty code we will skip all the checks.
6192   // we are just trying to get the call to be generated.
6193   Node* src_start  = src;
6194   Node* dest_start = dest;
6195   if (src_offset != NULL || dest_offset != NULL) {
6196     assert(src_offset != NULL && dest_offset != NULL, "");
6197     src_start  = array_element_address(src,  src_offset,  T_BYTE);
6198     dest_start = array_element_address(dest, dest_offset, T_BYTE);
6199   }
6200 
6201   // now need to get the start of its expanded key array
6202   // this requires a newer class file that has this array as littleEndian ints, otherwise we revert to java
6203   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6204   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
6205 
6206   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
6207     // on SPARC we need to pass the original key since key expansion needs to happen in intrinsics due to
6208     // compatibility issues between Java key expansion and SPARC crypto instructions
6209     Node* original_k_start = get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6210     if (original_k_start == NULL) return false;
6211 
6212     // Call the stub.
6213     make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::aescrypt_block_Type(),
6214                       stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6215                       src_start, dest_start, k_start, original_k_start);
6216   } else {
6217     // Call the stub.
6218     make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::aescrypt_block_Type(),
6219                       stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6220                       src_start, dest_start, k_start);
6221   }
6222 
6223   return true;
6224 }
6225 
6226 //------------------------------inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt-----------------------
6227 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6228   address stubAddr = NULL;
6229   const char *stubName = NULL;
6230 
6231   assert(UseAES, "need AES instruction support");
6232 
6233   switch(id) {
6234   case vmIntrinsics::_cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt:
6235     stubAddr = StubRoutines::cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt();
6236     stubName = "cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt";
6237     break;
6238   case vmIntrinsics::_cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt:
6239     stubAddr = StubRoutines::cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt();
6240     stubName = "cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt";
6241     break;
6242   default:
6243     break;
6244   }
6245   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6246 
6247   Node* cipherBlockChaining_object = argument(0);
6248   Node* src                        = argument(1);
6249   Node* src_offset                 = argument(2);
6250   Node* len                        = argument(3);
6251   Node* dest                       = argument(4);
6252   Node* dest_offset                = argument(5);
6253 
6254   src = must_be_not_null(src, false);
6255   dest = must_be_not_null(dest, false);
6256 
6257   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
6258   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6259   const Type* dest_type = dest->Value(&_gvn);
6260   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6261   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
6262   assert (top_src  != NULL && top_src->klass()  != NULL
6263           &&  top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL, "args are strange");
6264 
6265   // checks are the responsibility of the caller
6266   Node* src_start  = src;
6267   Node* dest_start = dest;
6268   if (src_offset != NULL || dest_offset != NULL) {
6269     assert(src_offset != NULL && dest_offset != NULL, "");
6270     src_start  = array_element_address(src,  src_offset,  T_BYTE);
6271     dest_start = array_element_address(dest, dest_offset, T_BYTE);
6272   }
6273 
6274   // if we are in this set of code, we "know" the embeddedCipher is an AESCrypt object
6275   // (because of the predicated logic executed earlier).
6276   // so we cast it here safely.
6277   // this requires a newer class file that has this array as littleEndian ints, otherwise we revert to java
6278 
6279   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(cipherBlockChaining_object, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6280   if (embeddedCipherObj == NULL) return false;
6281 
6282   // cast it to what we know it will be at runtime
6283   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(cipherBlockChaining_object)->isa_instptr();
6284   assert(tinst != NULL, "CBC obj is null");
6285   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "CBC obj is not loaded");
6286   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6287   assert(klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded(), "predicate checks that this class is loaded");
6288 
6289   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6290   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt);
6291   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
6292   Node* aescrypt_object = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), embeddedCipherObj, xtype);
6293   aescrypt_object = _gvn.transform(aescrypt_object);
6294 
6295   // we need to get the start of the aescrypt_object's expanded key array
6296   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6297   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
6298 
6299   // similarly, get the start address of the r vector
6300   Node* objRvec = load_field_from_object(cipherBlockChaining_object, "r", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6301   if (objRvec == NULL) return false;
6302   Node* r_start = array_element_address(objRvec, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6303 
6304   Node* cbcCrypt;
6305   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
6306     // on SPARC we need to pass the original key since key expansion needs to happen in intrinsics due to
6307     // compatibility issues between Java key expansion and SPARC crypto instructions
6308     Node* original_k_start = get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6309     if (original_k_start == NULL) return false;
6310 
6311     // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start, src_len and original_k_start
6312     cbcCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6313                                  OptoRuntime::cipherBlockChaining_aescrypt_Type(),
6314                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6315                                  src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start, len, original_k_start);
6316   } else {
6317     // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start and src_len
6318     cbcCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6319                                  OptoRuntime::cipherBlockChaining_aescrypt_Type(),
6320                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6321                                  src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start, len);
6322   }
6323 
6324   // return cipher length (int)
6325   Node* retvalue = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(cbcCrypt, TypeFunc::Parms));
6326   set_result(retvalue);
6327   return true;
6328 }

6418 //------------------------------inline_counterMode_AESCrypt-----------------------

6431   Node* counterMode_object = argument(0);

6433   Node* src_offset = argument(2);
6434   Node* len = argument(3);
6435   Node* dest = argument(4);
6436   Node* dest_offset = argument(5);
6437 
6438   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
6439   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6440   const Type* dest_type = dest->Value(&_gvn);
6441   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6442   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
6443   assert(top_src != NULL && top_src->klass() != NULL &&
6444          top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL, "args are strange");
6445 
6446   // checks are the responsibility of the caller
6447   Node* src_start = src;
6448   Node* dest_start = dest;
6449   if (src_offset != NULL || dest_offset != NULL) {
6450     assert(src_offset != NULL && dest_offset != NULL, "");
6451     src_start = array_element_address(src, src_offset, T_BYTE);
6452     dest_start = array_element_address(dest, dest_offset, T_BYTE);
6453   }
6454 
6455   // if we are in this set of code, we "know" the embeddedCipher is an AESCrypt object
6456   // (because of the predicated logic executed earlier).
6457   // so we cast it here safely.
6458   // this requires a newer class file that has this array as littleEndian ints, otherwise we revert to java
6459   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(counterMode_object, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);

6463   assert(tinst != NULL, "CTR obj is null");
6464   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "CTR obj is not loaded");
6465   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6466   assert(klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded(), "predicate checks that this class is loaded");
6467   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6468   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt);
6469   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
6470   Node* aescrypt_object = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), embeddedCipherObj, xtype);
6471   aescrypt_object = _gvn.transform(aescrypt_object);
6472   // we need to get the start of the aescrypt_object's expanded key array
6473   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6474   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
6475   // similarly, get the start address of the r vector
6476   Node* obj_counter = load_field_from_object(counterMode_object, "counter", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6477   if (obj_counter == NULL) return false;
6478   Node* cnt_start = array_element_address(obj_counter, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6479 
6480   Node* saved_encCounter = load_field_from_object(counterMode_object, "encryptedCounter", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6481   if (saved_encCounter == NULL) return false;
6482   Node* saved_encCounter_start = array_element_address(saved_encCounter, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6483   Node* used = field_address_from_object(counterMode_object, "used", "I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6484 
6485   Node* ctrCrypt;
6486   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
6487     // no SPARC version for AES/CTR intrinsics now.
6488     return false;
6489   }
6490   // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start and src_len
6491   ctrCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6492                                OptoRuntime::counterMode_aescrypt_Type(),
6493                                stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6494                                src_start, dest_start, k_start, cnt_start, len, saved_encCounter_start, used);
6495 
6496   // return cipher length (int)
6497   Node* retvalue = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(ctrCrypt, TypeFunc::Parms));
6498   set_result(retvalue);
6499   return true;
6500 }
6501 
6502 //------------------------------get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object-----------------------
6503 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(Node *aescrypt_object) {
6504 #if defined(PPC64) || defined(S390)
6505   // MixColumns for decryption can be reduced by preprocessing MixColumns with round keys.
6506   // Intel's extention is based on this optimization and AESCrypt generates round keys by preprocessing MixColumns.
6507   // However, ppc64 vncipher processes MixColumns and requires the same round keys with encryption.
6508   // The ppc64 stubs of encryption and decryption use the same round keys (sessionK[0]).
6509   Node* objSessionK = load_field_from_object(aescrypt_object, "sessionK", "[[I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6510   assert (objSessionK != NULL, "wrong version of com.sun.crypto.provider.AESCrypt");
6511   if (objSessionK == NULL) {
6512     return (Node *) NULL;
6513   }
6514   Node* objAESCryptKey = load_array_element(control(), objSessionK, intcon(0), TypeAryPtr::OOPS);
6515 #else
6516   Node* objAESCryptKey = load_field_from_object(aescrypt_object, "K", "[I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6517 #endif // PPC64
6518   assert (objAESCryptKey != NULL, "wrong version of com.sun.crypto.provider.AESCrypt");
6519   if (objAESCryptKey == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6520 
6521   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the K array
6522   Node* k_start = array_element_address(objAESCryptKey, intcon(0), T_INT);
6523   return k_start;
6524 }
6525 
6526 //------------------------------get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object-----------------------
6527 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(Node *aescrypt_object) {
6528   Node* objAESCryptKey = load_field_from_object(aescrypt_object, "lastKey", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6529   assert (objAESCryptKey != NULL, "wrong version of com.sun.crypto.provider.AESCrypt");
6530   if (objAESCryptKey == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6531 
6532   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the lastKey array
6533   Node* original_k_start = array_element_address(objAESCryptKey, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6534   return original_k_start;
6535 }
6536 
6537 //----------------------------inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt_predicate----------------------------
6538 // Return node representing slow path of predicate check.
6539 // the pseudo code we want to emulate with this predicate is:
6540 // for encryption:
6541 //    if (embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6542 // for decryption:
6543 //    if ((embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) && (cipher!=plain)) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6544 //    note cipher==plain is more conservative than the original java code but that's OK
6545 //
6546 Node* LibraryCallKit::inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt_predicate(bool decrypting) {
6547   // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6548   Node* objCBC = argument(0);
6549 
6550   Node* src = argument(1);
6551   Node* dest = argument(4);
6552 
6553   // Load embeddedCipher field of CipherBlockChaining object.
6554   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(objCBC, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6555 
6556   // get AESCrypt klass for instanceOf check
6557   // AESCrypt might not be loaded yet if some other SymmetricCipher got us to this compile point
6558   // will have same classloader as CipherBlockChaining object
6559   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(objCBC)->isa_instptr();
6560   assert(tinst != NULL, "CBCobj is null");
6561   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "CBCobj is not loaded");
6562 
6563   // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the AESCrypt class
6564   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6565   if (!klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded()) {
6566     // if AESCrypt is not even loaded, we never take the intrinsic fast path
6567     Node* ctrl = control();
6568     set_control(top()); // no regular fast path
6569     return ctrl;
6570   }
6571 
6572   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
6573   dest = must_be_not_null(dest, true);
6574 
6575   // Resolve oops to stable for CmpP below.
6576   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6577 
6578   Node* instof = gen_instanceof(embeddedCipherObj, makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt)));
6579   Node* cmp_instof  = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(instof, intcon(1)));
6580   Node* bool_instof  = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_instof, BoolTest::ne));
6581 
6582   Node* instof_false = generate_guard(bool_instof, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6583 
6584   // for encryption, we are done
6585   if (!decrypting)
6586     return instof_false;  // even if it is NULL
6587 
6588   // for decryption, we need to add a further check to avoid
6589   // taking the intrinsic path when cipher and plain are the same
6590   // see the original java code for why.
6591   RegionNode* region = new RegionNode(3);
6592   region->init_req(1, instof_false);
6593 
6594   Node* cmp_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new CmpPNode(src, dest));
6595   Node* bool_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_src_dest, BoolTest::eq));
6596   Node* src_dest_conjoint = generate_guard(bool_src_dest, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6597   region->init_req(2, src_dest_conjoint);
6598 
6599   record_for_igvn(region);
6600   return _gvn.transform(region);
6601 }

6603 //----------------------------inline_electronicCodeBook_AESCrypt_predicate----------------------------
6604 // Return node representing slow path of predicate check.
6605 // the pseudo code we want to emulate with this predicate is:
6606 // for encryption:
6607 //    if (embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6608 // for decryption:
6609 //    if ((embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) && (cipher!=plain)) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6610 //    note cipher==plain is more conservative than the original java code but that's OK
6611 //
6612 Node* LibraryCallKit::inline_electronicCodeBook_AESCrypt_predicate(bool decrypting) {

6617   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(objECB, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6618 
6619   // get AESCrypt klass for instanceOf check

6621   // will have same classloader as ElectronicCodeBook object

6628   if (!klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded()) {
6629     // if AESCrypt is not even loaded, we never take the intrinsic fast path
6630     Node* ctrl = control();
6631     set_control(top()); // no regular fast path
6632     return ctrl;
6633   }
6634   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6635 
6636   Node* instof = gen_instanceof(embeddedCipherObj, makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt)));
6637   Node* cmp_instof = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(instof, intcon(1)));
6638   Node* bool_instof = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_instof, BoolTest::ne));

6641

6643   if (!decrypting)
6644     return instof_false;  // even if it is NULL
6645 
6646   // for decryption, we need to add a further check to avoid
6647   // taking the intrinsic path when cipher and plain are the same
6648   // see the original java code for why.
6649   RegionNode* region = new RegionNode(3);
6650   region->init_req(1, instof_false);
6651   Node* src = argument(1);
6652   Node* dest = argument(4);

6656   region->init_req(2, src_dest_conjoint);
6657 
6658   record_for_igvn(region);
6659   return _gvn.transform(region);
6660 }

6704 //------------------------------inline_ghash_processBlocks
6705 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_ghash_processBlocks() {

6708   assert(UseGHASHIntrinsics, "need GHASH intrinsics support");
6709

6715   Node* len            = argument(2);

6722

6731                                   OptoRuntime::ghash_processBlocks_Type(),
