6769 //------------------------------inline_sha_implCompress-----------------------
6770 //
6771 // Calculate SHA (i.e., SHA-1) for single-block byte[] array.
6772 // void com.sun.security.provider.SHA.implCompress(byte[] buf, int ofs)
6773 //
6774 // Calculate SHA2 (i.e., SHA-244 or SHA-256) for single-block byte[] array.
6775 // void com.sun.security.provider.SHA2.implCompress(byte[] buf, int ofs)
6776 //
6777 // Calculate SHA5 (i.e., SHA-384 or SHA-512) for single-block byte[] array.
6778 // void com.sun.security.provider.SHA5.implCompress(byte[] buf, int ofs)
6779 //
6780 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_sha_implCompress(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6781   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 2, "sha_implCompress has 2 parameters");
6782 
6783   Node* sha_obj = argument(0);
6784   Node* src     = argument(1); // type oop
6785   Node* ofs     = argument(2); // type int
6786 
6787   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6788   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6789   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
6790     // failed array check
6791     return false;
6792   }
6793   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
6794   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
6795   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
6796     return false;
6797   }
6798   // 'src_start' points to src array + offset
6799   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
6800   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, ofs, src_elem);
6801   Node* state = NULL;
6802   address stubAddr;
6803   const char *stubName;
6804 
6805   switch(id) {
6806   case vmIntrinsics::_sha_implCompress:
6807     assert(UseSHA1Intrinsics, "need SHA1 instruction support");
6808     state = get_state_from_sha_object(sha_obj);
6809     stubAddr = StubRoutines::sha1_implCompress();
6810     stubName = "sha1_implCompress";
6811     break;
6812   case vmIntrinsics::_sha2_implCompress:
6813     assert(UseSHA256Intrinsics, "need SHA256 instruction support");
6814     state = get_state_from_sha_object(sha_obj);
6815     stubAddr = StubRoutines::sha256_implCompress();
6816     stubName = "sha256_implCompress";
6817     break;
6818   case vmIntrinsics::_sha5_implCompress:
6819     assert(UseSHA512Intrinsics, "need SHA512 instruction support");
6820     state = get_state_from_sha5_object(sha_obj);
6821     stubAddr = StubRoutines::sha512_implCompress();
6822     stubName = "sha512_implCompress";
6823     break;
6824   default:
6825     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
6826     return false;
6827   }
6828   if (state == NULL) return false;
6829 
6830   assert(stubAddr != NULL, "Stub is generated");
6831   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6832 
6833   // Call the stub.
6834   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::sha_implCompress_Type(),
6835                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6836                                  src_start, state);
6837 
6838   return true;
6839 }
6840 
6841 //------------------------------inline_digestBase_implCompressMB-----------------------
6842 //
6843 // Calculate SHA/SHA2/SHA5 for multi-block byte[] array.
6844 // int com.sun.security.provider.DigestBase.implCompressMultiBlock(byte[] b, int ofs, int limit)
6845 //
6846 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_digestBase_implCompressMB(int predicate) {
6847   assert(UseSHA1Intrinsics || UseSHA256Intrinsics || UseSHA512Intrinsics,
6848          "need SHA1/SHA256/SHA512 instruction support");
6849   assert((uint)predicate < 3, "sanity");
6850   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 3, "digestBase_implCompressMB has 3 parameters");
6851 
6852   Node* digestBase_obj = argument(0); // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6853   Node* src            = argument(1); // byte[] array
6854   Node* ofs            = argument(2); // type int
6855   Node* limit          = argument(3); // type int
6856 
6857   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6858   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6859   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
6860     // failed array check
6861     return false;
6862   }
6863   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
6864   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
6865   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
6866     return false;
6867   }
6868   // 'src_start' points to src array + offset
6869   src = must_be_not_null(src, false);
6870   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, ofs, src_elem);
6871 
6872   const char* klass_SHA_name = NULL;
6873   const char* stub_name = NULL;
6874   address     stub_addr = NULL;
6875   bool        long_state = false;
6876 
6877   switch (predicate) {
6878   case 0:
6879     if (UseSHA1Intrinsics) {
6880       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA";
6881       stub_name = "sha1_implCompressMB";
6882       stub_addr = StubRoutines::sha1_implCompressMB();
6883     }
6884     break;
6885   case 1:
6886     if (UseSHA256Intrinsics) {
6887       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA2";
6888       stub_name = "sha256_implCompressMB";
6889       stub_addr = StubRoutines::sha256_implCompressMB();
6890     }
6891     break;
6892   case 2:
6893     if (UseSHA512Intrinsics) {
6894       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA5";
6895       stub_name = "sha512_implCompressMB";
6896       stub_addr = StubRoutines::sha512_implCompressMB();
6897       long_state = true;
6898     }
6899     break;
6900   default:
6901     fatal("unknown SHA intrinsic predicate: %d", predicate);
6902   }
6903   if (klass_SHA_name != NULL) {
6904     assert(stub_addr != NULL, "Stub is generated");
6905     if (stub_addr == NULL) return false;
6906 
6907     // get DigestBase klass to lookup for SHA klass
6908     const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(digestBase_obj)->isa_instptr();
6909     assert(tinst != NULL, "digestBase_obj is not instance???");
6910     assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "DigestBase is not loaded");
6911 
6912     ciKlass* klass_SHA = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make(klass_SHA_name));
6913     assert(klass_SHA->is_loaded(), "predicate checks that this class is loaded");
6914     ciInstanceKlass* instklass_SHA = klass_SHA->as_instance_klass();
6915     return inline_sha_implCompressMB(digestBase_obj, instklass_SHA, long_state, stub_addr, stub_name, src_start, ofs, limit);
6916   }
6917   return false;
6918 }
6919 //------------------------------inline_sha_implCompressMB-----------------------
6920 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_sha_implCompressMB(Node* digestBase_obj, ciInstanceKlass* instklass_SHA,
6921                                                bool long_state, address stubAddr, const char *stubName,
6922                                                Node* src_start, Node* ofs, Node* limit) {
6923   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_SHA);
6924   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
6925   Node* sha_obj = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), digestBase_obj, xtype);
6926   sha_obj = _gvn.transform(sha_obj);
6927 
6928   Node* state;
6929   if (long_state) {
6930     state = get_state_from_sha5_object(sha_obj);
6931   } else {
6932     state = get_state_from_sha_object(sha_obj);
6933   }
6934   if (state == NULL) return false;
6935 
6936   // Call the stub.
6937   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6938                                  OptoRuntime::digestBase_implCompressMB_Type(),
6939                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6940                                  src_start, state, ofs, limit);
6941   // return ofs (int)
6942   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
6943   set_result(result);
6944 
6945   return true;
6946 }
6947 
6948 //------------------------------get_state_from_sha_object-----------------------
6949 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_state_from_sha_object(Node *sha_object) {
6950   Node* sha_state = load_field_from_object(sha_object, "state", "[I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6951   assert (sha_state != NULL, "wrong version of sun.security.provider.SHA/SHA2");
6952   if (sha_state == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6953 
6954   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the state array
6955   Node* state = array_element_address(sha_state, intcon(0), T_INT);
6956   return state;
6957 }
6958 
6959 //------------------------------get_state_from_sha5_object-----------------------
6960 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_state_from_sha5_object(Node *sha_object) {
6961   Node* sha_state = load_field_from_object(sha_object, "state", "[J", /*is_exact*/ false);
6962   assert (sha_state != NULL, "wrong version of sun.security.provider.SHA5");
6963   if (sha_state == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6964 
6965   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the state array
6966   Node* state = array_element_address(sha_state, intcon(0), T_LONG);
6967   return state;
6968 }
6969 
6970 //----------------------------inline_digestBase_implCompressMB_predicate----------------------------
6971 // Return node representing slow path of predicate check.
6972 // the pseudo code we want to emulate with this predicate is:
6973 //    if (digestBaseObj instanceof SHA/SHA2/SHA5) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6974 //
6975 Node* LibraryCallKit::inline_digestBase_implCompressMB_predicate(int predicate) {
6976   assert(UseSHA1Intrinsics || UseSHA256Intrinsics || UseSHA512Intrinsics,
6977          "need SHA1/SHA256/SHA512 instruction support");
6978   assert((uint)predicate < 3, "sanity");
6979 
6980   // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6981   Node* digestBaseObj = argument(0);
6982 
6983   // get DigestBase klass for instanceOf check
6984   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(digestBaseObj)->isa_instptr();
6985   assert(tinst != NULL, "digestBaseObj is null");
6986   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "DigestBase is not loaded");
6987 
6988   const char* klass_SHA_name = NULL;
6989   switch (predicate) {
6990   case 0:
6991     if (UseSHA1Intrinsics) {
6992       // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the SHA class
6993       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA";
6994     }
6995     break;
6996   case 1:
6997     if (UseSHA256Intrinsics) {
6998       // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the SHA2 class
6999       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA2";
7000     }
7001     break;
7002   case 2:
7003     if (UseSHA512Intrinsics) {
7004       // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the SHA5 class
7005       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA5";
7006     }
7007     break;
7008   default:
7009     fatal("unknown SHA intrinsic predicate: %d", predicate);
7010   }
7011 
7012   ciKlass* klass_SHA = NULL;
7013   if (klass_SHA_name != NULL) {
7014     klass_SHA = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make(klass_SHA_name));
7015   }
7016   if ((klass_SHA == NULL) || !klass_SHA->is_loaded()) {
7017     // if none of SHA/SHA2/SHA5 is loaded, we never take the intrinsic fast path
7018     Node* ctrl = control();
7019     set_control(top()); // no intrinsic path
7020     return ctrl;
7021   }
7022   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_SHA = klass_SHA->as_instance_klass();
7023 
7024   Node* instofSHA = gen_instanceof(digestBaseObj, makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_SHA)));
7025   Node* cmp_instof = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(instofSHA, intcon(1)));
7026   Node* bool_instof = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_instof, BoolTest::ne));
7027   Node* instof_false = generate_guard(bool_instof, NULL, PROB_MIN);
7028 
7029   return instof_false;  // even if it is NULL
7030 }
7031 
7032 //-------------inline_fma-----------------------------------
7033 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_fma(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
7034   Node *a = NULL;
7035   Node *b = NULL;
7036   Node *c = NULL;
7037   Node* result = NULL;
7038   switch (id) {
7039   case vmIntrinsics::_fmaD:
7040     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 6, "fma has 3 parameters of size 2 each.");
7041     // no receiver since it is static method
7042     a = round_double_node(argument(0));
7043     b = round_double_node(argument(2));
7044     c = round_double_node(argument(4));
7045     result = _gvn.transform(new FmaDNode(control(), a, b, c));
7046     break;
7047   case vmIntrinsics::_fmaF:
7048     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 3, "fma has 3 parameters of size 1 each.");
7049     a = argument(0);
7050     b = argument(1);
7051     c = argument(2);
7052     result = _gvn.transform(new FmaFNode(control(), a, b, c));
7053     break;
7054   default:
7055     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);  break;
7056   }
7057   set_result(result);
7058   return true;
7059 }
7060 
7061 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_character_compare(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
7062   // argument(0) is receiver
7063   Node* codePoint = argument(1);
7064   Node* n = NULL;
7065 
7066   switch (id) {
7067     case vmIntrinsics::_isDigit :
7068       n = new DigitNode(control(), codePoint);
7069       break;
7070     case vmIntrinsics::_isLowerCase :
7071       n = new LowerCaseNode(control(), codePoint);
7072       break;
7073     case vmIntrinsics::_isUpperCase :
7074       n = new UpperCaseNode(control(), codePoint);
7075       break;
7076     case vmIntrinsics::_isWhitespace :
7077       n = new WhitespaceNode(control(), codePoint);
7078       break;
7079     default:
7080       fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
7081   }
7082 
7083   set_result(_gvn.transform(n));
7084   return true;
7085 }
7086 
7087 //------------------------------inline_fp_min_max------------------------------
7088 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_fp_min_max(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
7089 /* DISABLED BECAUSE METHOD DATA ISN'T COLLECTED PER CALL-SITE, SEE JDK-8015416.
7090 
7091   // The intrinsic should be used only when the API branches aren't predictable,
7092   // the last one performing the most important comparison. The following heuristic
7093   // uses the branch statistics to eventually bail out if necessary.
7094 
7095   ciMethodData *md = callee()->method_data();
7096 
7097   if ( md != NULL && md->is_mature() && md->invocation_count() > 0 ) {
7098     ciCallProfile cp = caller()->call_profile_at_bci(bci());
7099 
7100     if ( ((double)cp.count()) / ((double)md->invocation_count()) < 0.8 ) {
7101       // Bail out if the call-site didn't contribute enough to the statistics.
7102       return false;
7103     }
7104 
7105     uint taken = 0, not_taken = 0;
7106 
7107     for (ciProfileData *p = md->first_data(); md->is_valid(p); p = md->next_data(p)) {
7108       if (p->is_BranchData()) {
7109         taken = ((ciBranchData*)p)->taken();
7110         not_taken = ((ciBranchData*)p)->not_taken();
7111       }
7112     }
7113 
7114     double balance = (((double)taken) - ((double)not_taken)) / ((double)md->invocation_count());
7115     balance = balance < 0 ? -balance : balance;
7116     if ( balance > 0.2 ) {
7117       // Bail out if the most important branch is predictable enough.
7118       return false;
7119     }
7120   }
7121 */
7122 
7123   Node *a = NULL;
7124   Node *b = NULL;
7125   Node *n = NULL;
7126   switch (id) {
7127   case vmIntrinsics::_maxF:
7128   case vmIntrinsics::_minF:
7129     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 2, "minF/maxF has 2 parameters of size 1 each.");
7130     a = argument(0);
7131     b = argument(1);
7132     break;
7133   case vmIntrinsics::_maxD:
7134   case vmIntrinsics::_minD:
7135     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "minD/maxD has 2 parameters of size 2 each.");
7136     a = round_double_node(argument(0));
7137     b = round_double_node(argument(2));
7138     break;
7139   default:
7140     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
7141     break;
7142   }
7143   switch (id) {
7144   case vmIntrinsics::_maxF:  n = new MaxFNode(a, b);  break;
7145   case vmIntrinsics::_minF:  n = new MinFNode(a, b);  break;
7146   case vmIntrinsics::_maxD:  n = new MaxDNode(a, b);  break;
7147   case vmIntrinsics::_minD:  n = new MinDNode(a, b);  break;
7148   default:  fatal_unexpected_iid(id);  break;
7149   }
7150   set_result(_gvn.transform(n));
7151   return true;
7152 }
7153 
7154 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_profileBoolean() {
7155   Node* counts = argument(1);
7156   const TypeAryPtr* ary = NULL;
7157   ciArray* aobj = NULL;
7158   if (counts->is_Con()
7159       && (ary = counts->bottom_type()->isa_aryptr()) != NULL
7160       && (aobj = ary->const_oop()->as_array()) != NULL
7161       && (aobj->length() == 2)) {
7162     // Profile is int[2] where [0] and [1] correspond to false and true value occurrences respectively.
7163     jint false_cnt = aobj->element_value(0).as_int();
7164     jint  true_cnt = aobj->element_value(1).as_int();
7165 
7166     if (C->log() != NULL) {
7167       C->log()->elem("observe source='profileBoolean' false='%d' true='%d'",
7168                      false_cnt, true_cnt);
7169     }
7170 
7171     if (false_cnt + true_cnt == 0) {
7172       // According to profile, never executed.
7173       uncommon_trap_exact(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
7174                           Deoptimization::Action_reinterpret);
7175       return true;
7176     }
7177 
7178     // result is a boolean (0 or 1) and its profile (false_cnt & true_cnt)
7179     // is a number of each value occurrences.
7180     Node* result = argument(0);
7181     if (false_cnt == 0 || true_cnt == 0) {
7182       // According to profile, one value has been never seen.
7183       int expected_val = (false_cnt == 0) ? 1 : 0;
7184 
7185       Node* cmp  = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(result, intcon(expected_val)));
7186       Node* test = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp, BoolTest::eq));
7187 
7188       IfNode* check = create_and_map_if(control(), test, PROB_ALWAYS, COUNT_UNKNOWN);
7189       Node* fast_path = _gvn.transform(new IfTrueNode(check));
7190       Node* slow_path = _gvn.transform(new IfFalseNode(check));
7191 
7192       { // Slow path: uncommon trap for never seen value and then reexecute
7193         // MethodHandleImpl::profileBoolean() to bump the count, so JIT knows
7194         // the value has been seen at least once.
7195         PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
7196         PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
7197         jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
7198 
7199         set_control(slow_path);
7200         set_i_o(i_o());
7201 
7202         uncommon_trap_exact(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
7203                             Deoptimization::Action_reinterpret);
7204       }
7205       // The guard for never seen value enables sharpening of the result and
7206       // returning a constant. It allows to eliminate branches on the same value
7207       // later on.
7208       set_control(fast_path);
7209       result = intcon(expected_val);
7210     }
7211     // Stop profiling.
7212     // MethodHandleImpl::profileBoolean() has profiling logic in its bytecode.
7213     // By replacing method body with profile data (represented as ProfileBooleanNode
7214     // on IR level) we effectively disable profiling.
7215     // It enables full speed execution once optimized code is generated.
7216     Node* profile = _gvn.transform(new ProfileBooleanNode(result, false_cnt, true_cnt));
7217     C->record_for_igvn(profile);
7218     set_result(profile);
7219     return true;
7220   } else {
7221     // Continue profiling.
7222     // Profile data isn't available at the moment. So, execute method's bytecode version.
7223     // Usually, when GWT LambdaForms are profiled it means that a stand-alone nmethod
7224     // is compiled and counters aren't available since corresponding MethodHandle
7225     // isn't a compile-time constant.
7226     return false;
7227   }
7228 }
7229 
7230 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_isCompileConstant() {
7231   Node* n = argument(0);
7232   set_result(n->is_Con() ? intcon(1) : intcon(0));
7233   return true;
7234 }
